<rating>5</rating><review>There are three places to enjoy the great view that Ansel Adams made famous:
1. From the parking lot just outside the Wawona Tunnel on the highway 41. This is the easiest and does not require any hiking.
2. From Artist Point on the old Wawona Road, which requires you to hike 2miles with an elevation of 500 feet.
3. From Inspiration Point on pohono trail, it is a 2.6 mile hike with an elevation of 950 feet.

Form all three places, you have the similar vista of El Capitan, Half Dome, and Bridalview Fall.
The reason people take the hike to artist point and inspiration point is there are far fewer people at these vista points.

The Artist Point trail started from the Tunnel View parking lot, the first half mile is the Pohono Trail (same for Inspiration Point Trail). It is a very steep incline and switchback.
You will gain 500 feet very quickly, Then you will meet the cross road of pohono and the old stagecoach road (i.e the old wawona road).  There are signs at cross road, just make a left turn at the intersection and you will be fine. Continue 0.5 mile you will reach the Artist Point (one more mile will send you to the bridalveil fall parking area where old wanowa road meets the new wawona road). The final 0.25 mile is all  downhill with about 200 feet elveation.

There is no sign of the point, but you can not miss it. If you are lucky, most likely you will be the only one at the spot. It is a great place to take some serious photos.
If you visit the place in April or May, do continue another 50 yards, you will see a small waterfall run cross the trail.<//review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM3AGwibatB8-C7lSy71xXS60X36qcknrMXLkYU=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMSmRJKxiSOk1csJi69l3TjzlrHe4E5BmNEiOAD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMxj_wMQuEXPPvxsRmrIPu127zaVB1z65OG3idL=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNjIN6l8gcPlCoWzkE59Ejm1ID4BVf3iqr1pHwb=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPsGym5er-9bfBsIlvdRwEwtcHVRH09BwI01-QO=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOk2CVjg4BSY7goNQM1IqIudhcALjRQ_8_d0UWu=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN3g2xN--bBf7-nhku7I4oLwSOSemCAcylwIgk-=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMa1OfP-3EtzBk9Oq_lco1I6NEGy9ewqeVL0Jf5=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOKy8n6EzlceU8IQb29gy-1855uB-_91GjnBKan=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMq41kkwqpGU0SuRGz9CXnUXf5rNWJ9HPw4JR91=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMZMN3v62GzXm-8r45eBfM6obnSrCRpQ1ZU3UsG=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOOUTnueqO8-cjlM4NQUj9TyMMlUsuiyIdAIwd-=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics>< Resp>

<Time>1507604977256</Time><rating>5<//rating><Review>This is a "real" hidden gem!   After exiting the Wawona Tunnel driving towards Yosemite Valley, turn into the left parking lot or the right side parking lot.  At Tunnel View, large crowds assemble for this outstanding view.  Try the right side parking lot if possible.  There, about half way down the parking lot, you will see some steps going up to the Pohono Trail.  This is the beginning of the Artist Point Trail.

The first 6/10 mile is fairly steep with some views of Yosemite Valley.  At 6/10 mile, you will come upon an old stagecoach road.   There will be a sign here pointing straight to continue to the Inspiration Point vista.  BUT, at this stagecoach road, turn LEFT (when we were there no sign was in place for Artist Point) and then descend a bit for 1/2 mile.   At some places you will have to climb over fallen trees.  You will definitely notice the Artist Point vista to the left with a steep uphill rock formation to the right.

There is a nice bench type rock for pictures and to rest.  Do this hike.  When we were there in September 2017, there was no one else there!  Outstanding views (without the crowds)!    View:  El Capitan, Cloud's Rest, Bridalveil Fall, Half Dome.  Elevation at parking lot:  4390'; elevation at Artist Point: 4701'.   The round-trip hike is 2.2 miles.    Highly recommended and a somewhat tough hiking going up for the first 6/10 mile of your hike.  Take some water and your camera!</Review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOQwmDHDIm4DO8PwQ7iLzK-4Lh_LsNnPqtSiWnj=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMLokP3pDmBNWmqIM6QG1zucjPpWwKUuKdh2uSp=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures>< response>

But the Artist Point has unobstructed views on the valley and were breathtaking. Highly recommend this hike for people that want to do a easy trail. We went mid June and there was no one else on the trail! Great time to come to Yosemite to get amazing weather and before the crowds arrive.</review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNIH0zn8-QBvw4wrN9jAOb0MZXdw_elk3XXnNkO=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< Rate>

The Artist Point is a lookout point on the edge of a cliff and just before the tunnel and was originally named in 1883 by Frank Jay Haynes, who wrongly believed that the place was where the painter Thomas Moran designed his representations of the waterfalls in 1872. Later work it was found that the sketches were made from the northern edge, but the name Artist Point was retained.
From there you can also start some hiking routes. One loop is about 5.5 km, which takes about 1.5 to 2 hours. Or you can take the larger one with about 34 km, where you should start earlier.
Since you can park well here and there are enough parking spaces here you can start very well with the hiking routes.
Or you can just look at the beautiful panorama from the other side of the street and see the waterfalls better in spring.</review><Response>None<//Response><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNDNQuDHAzRVrONSsioVE63oWEmdwtGLDelhngB=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPcAIrcERnTU2nE3HCvECh4EpwsEgEX5ZX5Ju8w=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMUB-HcUyfJTwOYLpYVwng9uVcJ6GWXpOd2uNIO=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP-KRs-r-pdlJ7gfp5C7mKupaPeWjYsg9QsqJhw=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOcV047n_pX0ysW3fzLNrFuF19w27ROtJ0ULmHJ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMxiEJRrJo8kf6iOQuRJn_EPI7QFR2uTCHMfHUs=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOZHaPgRMP6QVJdb_uzFlqX7lYLNRgqam7wbTgl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMYk49S4wr_sGvTMntfEswaMraTY38OKk31mMIB=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMJ96ghv-FKqwaJd7bK75FrqoMjmC-7YlJNs9W-=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics><date>1576473604429<//date></record>

Restaurant options are limited in the area so this is a  good place for a quick bite. The menu has alot of variety and things to choose from. I got a fried chicken taquitos plate and it came with rice, beans, lettuce, avocado, cream and hot sauce. Tasty and satisfying, I was not disappointed at all. I originally went for the pizza but when I saw all the options I quickly changed my mind, I am glad I did too. Definitely going back to try the chili cheese burger soon. I didn't realize that it was Cash Only so keep that in mind; there is a convenience store next door with an ATM which I ended up using. Overall I enjoy this lunch spot.<//review>

< Name>
Matt Brown</Name>
< Text>
In a national contest to determine the best ice cream destination in the country, Shubert's came in second. They were robbed. Shubert's has been around for over 100 years, and Shubert's makes some of, if not the very best ice cream on the planet. Every item, even their chocolate dipped Oreos are fresh, delicious, and if you're lucky enough to catch the fresh boysenberry sundaes in season then you're going to have an experience rare to duplicate in this world. Shubert's also does candies and chocolates, and if you want to treat your mom, Dad, or sweet with a delicious box of sweets for Christmas, Easter or Valentine's Day, Shubert's should be your number one destination. Seriously, I can't recommend this place enough. Delicious!<//Text>

Excellent ice cream, my favorite is the seasonal peach, but my family LOVES the Mount Shasta flavor. Honestly, I've yet to encounter an ice cream here that isn't fantastic. There's frequently a line right out the door, so be prepared to wait a bit for your frozen treats, it's worth it. Their iced tea is great, but request easy ice, it's brimfull. Always worth a trip.<//Review>

Most famous for their Chico mint flavor, which is delicious! 1623817884237</time>
< Rate>
5</Rate>
< Review>
I went there with a purpose. My Pops and I shop in Chico, and for the 2 years he's been wanting to go to Schubert's after we finish shopping before we head up the hill toward Magalia. He likes the Maple Walnut  because hes from Massachusetts and he use to get that flavor growing up as a child a lot. He loved it. But  because we go to 2 different stores and usually have a lot of perushables, we tend to say "next time" and go home.

My Pops is 90, and was hospitalized at Enloe recently for 2 weeks. He wasn't eating very much, so I drove over to Shuberts, got him a quart and he ate half of it. He was thrilled.  Schubert's Maple Walnut was the last dessert he ate.  He died on Friday.  Thank you Shuberts for the Maple Walnut. You made a dying man's day. I just know he's up there bragging about it.</Review>
